        <div class="elementskit-infobox text-left text- icon-lef-right-aligin elementor-animation-   ">
                        <div class="box-body">
                            <h3 class="elementskit-info-box-title">
                    Welcome to the FREAK SHOW!                </h3>
                        		  	<p>Welcome to the FREAK SHOW Horror Film Festival, the largest horror genre film festival in Orlando, Florida. Our aim is to offer a platform to the finest independent horror films worldwide and celebrate their creators. While many film festivals neglect the horror genre, we offer filmmakers and enthusiasts an opportunity to view and exhibit movies that they may not get to see on the big screen.</p>
